### [81] [A Composite Theory of Higgs and Flavour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19650)
*Joe Davighi,Gino Isidori*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种复合希格斯模型，通过味解构规范群嵌入强相互作用扇区，利用全局对称性破缺产生多个赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子（pNGB），包括标准模型希格斯、破缺味非普适规范群的link场，以及仅耦合轻代费米子的第二希格斯二重态；该重希格斯自然导致受抑的轻夸克Yukawa耦合，从而解决味等级问题，同时新物理对味破坏观测量的贡献被CKM矩阵和手征性压低，电偶极矩限制也因轻费米子质量自动对齐而规避；该框架自然地统一解释希格斯与味等级起源，减小希格斯质量调谐，并最小化对味观测量的影响，主要可通过高动量转移与精确电弱测量进行检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决标准模型中希格斯质量和味结构的等级问题（flavour puzzle），并协调新物理对 flavour violating observables 和电偶极矩的实验约束。

Method: 构建一个包含味解构规范群的复合希格斯模型，使强相互作用扇区发生特定模式的全局对称性破缺，生成多个赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子（pNGB），其中包含SM希格斯、link场及第二希格斯二重态；利用其耦合结构实现轻代Yukawa耦合的压制，并借助CKM与手征抑制及质量自动对齐机制规避味破坏与EDM实验限制。

Result: 获得一个能同时解释希格斯与味等级起源的自然框架：希格斯质量调谐减小、味观测量影响最小化、电偶极矩界限自动满足；新物理效应主要体现于高pT过程与电弱精密测量。

Conclusion: 该模型为统一解决希格斯层级问题与味等级问题提供了自洽且实验上可检验的新机制，在保持与现有 flavour 和 EDM 实验一致的同时，显著降低了理论调谐度。

Abstract: We introduce a composite Higgs model in which a flavour deconstructed gauge group is embedded in the strong sector. The pattern of global symmetry breaking yields, as pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone (pNGB) bosons, both a Standard Model (SM)-like Higgs and the link field whose vacuum expectation value breaks the flavour non-universal gauge group down to the SM. Inevitably, a third pNGB appears, transforming as a second Higgs doublet coupled only to the light generations. This heavy Higgs naturally mediates suppressed light Yukawa couplings, providing a solution to the flavour puzzle. At the same time, new physics contributions to flavour violating observables are CKM- and chirally suppressed, while electric dipole moment bounds are evaded through an automatic mass alignment in the light fermion sector. The result is a natural framework for addressing the origin of both Higgs and flavour hierarchies, with reduced Higgs mass tuning and minimised impact in flavour observables, that is best tested by high-$p_T$ and precision electroweak measurements.

### [82] [The Clustering of Little Red Dots from Ultra-Strongly Self-Interacting Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18000)
*M. Grant Roberts,Aarna Garg,Tesla Jeltema,Stefano Profumo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文预测了由超强自相互作用暗物质（uSIDM）孕育的“小红点”（LRDs）在z~5处的有效成团偏置参数b_eff≈4.5，对应典型宿主晕质量约8×10^10 M⊙，且该预测对uSIDM微观参数不敏感，可被JWST观测检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解释高红移‘小红点’（LRDs）的观测特性，特别是其质量函数，并探索其可能起源于超强力自相互作用暗物质（uSIDM）这一新机制，需对其大尺度成团性（即偏置参数）作出可检验的理论预言。

Method: 基于uSIDM模型构建LRDs的形成框架，结合晕统计与偏置理论，计算其在红移z∼5处的有效成团偏置参数b_eff，并分析其对uSIDM微物理参数（如σ/m和分数f）的依赖性。

Result: 预测LRDs由uSIDM孕育时，其有效偏置b_eff≈4.5，对应宿主晕质量约8×10^10 M⊙；该结果与高红移类星体显著不同，且对uSIDM的截面σ/m和成分分数f等参数不敏感，具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 这是首个与LRDs质量函数一致、基于形成机制的成团性理论预测；其鲁棒性使即将开展的JWST观测能直接检验uSIDM是否为LRDs的真实起源。

Abstract: We predict the effective clustering bias parameter, $b_{\rm{eff}}$, at $z\sim5$ for Little Red Dots (LRDs) seeded by Ultra-Strongly Self-Interacting Dark Matter (uSIDM). From our model, we find that $b_{\rm{eff}}\sim4.5$, thus we infer that LRDs seeded by uSIDM would populate halos of typical masses $\sim 8\times10^{10}~M_{\odot}$; this bias factor is consistent with LRDs being a distinct population from high redshift quasars. To the extent that we are aware, this is the first formation-based theoretical prediction of LRD clustering from a model consistent with the LRD mass function. We find that this bias and clustering is insensitive to a wide range of the underlying uSIDM microphysics parameters, including the uSIDM cross-section $σ/m$ and uSIDM fraction $f$. This is therefore a robust prediction from the uSIDM model, and will allow for direct probes of the uSIDM paradigm as the origin of LRDs in the next few years. Upcoming \texttt{JWST} observations will constrain the population of LRDs, including directly measuring their clustering.

### [83] [Harmony of the Spheres: Extension to All Points of an Algorithm for Producing a Density Field with Given Two-, Three-, and Four-Point Correlation Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18547)
*Zcahary Slepian,Alessandro Greco*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文扩展了Smith-Zaldarriaga算法，使其能生成在网格上每一点都满足任意指定N点相关函数（NPCFs）的三维密度场，从而将‘约束实现’方法推广至高阶统计量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前算法仅保证在特定‘主点’处满足指定N点相关函数；本文旨在实现对网格上所有点均满足目标NPCFs的更普适构造。

Method: 基于Slepian (2024) 对Smith-Zaldarriaga (2011) 算法的初步推广，进一步证明并实现该算法可严格满足以网格上任意点为参考中心的N点相关函数要求。

Result: 成功构建出在整张网格上每一点均精确复现任意指定2点、3点……N点相关函数的三维密度场；完成对Hoffman & Ribak (1991) ‘约束实现’框架向高阶统计的完整推广。

Conclusion: 该算法为大尺度结构巡天（如DESI、Euclid、SPHEREx、Roman）提供了一种快速生成具有精确高阶统计特性的模拟密度场的有效工具，可用于协方差估计与系统误差检验。

Abstract: Previous work (Slepian 2024) showed that the Smith-Zaldarriaga (2011) algorithm to realize Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) maps with any desired harmonic-space bispectrum could be generalized to produce a 3D density field with any desired N-Point Correlation Functions (NPCFs, N = $2, 3, \ldots$) about a particular, specified set of ``primary'' points. This algorithm assured one of having the correct correlations if measured about these specific centers. Here, we show that this algorithm was more general than initially believed, and can in fact be used to produce a density field on a grid that has the correct, desired NPCFs as measured about \textit{every} point on the grid. This paper should be considered the second in the series, and now completes the quest to generalize the idea of ``constrained realization'' (Hoffman and Ribak 1991) to higher-order statistics. This algorithm will be of great use for quickly generating density fields both to produce covariance matrices, and test systematics, for current and future 3D large-scale structure surveys such as Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI), Euclid, Spherex, and Roman.

</details>


### [84] [Nanohertz Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18822)
*Alberto Sesana,Daniel G. Figueroa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）探测到的纳赫兹引力波信号的物理起源，重点分析了天体物理（如大质量黑洞并合）和宇宙学（如暴胀、相变、拓扑缺陷）来源的引力波背景，并指出其对天体物理与粒子物理的深远意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PTA数据中出现引力波信号证据，亟需理解其物理起源，区分天体物理与宇宙学机制，并探索其对基础物理的启示。

Method: 系统梳理和比较不同引力波背景（天体物理MBHB并合、暴胀、一级相变、拓扑缺陷等）的产生机制、频谱特征及可观测效应，并评估PTA对其约束能力。

Result: 确认纳赫兹引力波背景可源于多种机制；环境耦合、偏心率和采样稀疏性显著影响天体物理信号预测；PTA为检验超越标准模型的高能物理提供了新探针。

Conclusion: PTA引力波探测开启了纳赫兹宇宙学新窗口，有望同时深化对黑洞并合、早期宇宙演化、暗物质及奇异天体（如原初黑洞、宇宙弦）的理解。

Abstract: Evidence of a gravitational wave (GW) signal has emerged in pulsar timing array (PTA) data, opening a new window into the nanoHz GW Universe. We explore the physics of GW signals potentially explaining the data, with a primary focus on GW backgrounds (GWBs), considering both astrophysical and cosmological origins. We describe how: (i) An astrophysical nanoHz GWB emerges as the superposition of individual signals from inspiralling massive black-hole binaries (MBHBs); (ii) Environment coupling, eccentricity, and sparse sampling, affect the MBHB signal spectrum and statistical properties, causing great uncertainty in theoretical predictions, but simultaneously offering a handle to discriminate a potential astrophysical origin; (iii) PTA data offers unprecedented opportunities to constrain high-energy physics beyond the standard model, by probing early Universe GWBs, originated during or after inflation; (iv) Different early Universe GWBs, typically created by non-linear and out-of-equilibrium dynamics, can explain the PTA data, as e.g. from inflation scenarios, first order phase transitions, or topological defects; (v) The PTA detection of GWs opens a new window to explore the Universe, with profound implications for astrophysics and particle physics, probing e.g. the equation of state of the early Universe, the origin of the cosmological perturbations, the nature of the dark matter, or whether exotic objects like primordial black holes or cosmic strings exist.

</details>


### [85] [Constraints on the polarization angle oscillations of the Crab Nebula with the Simons Array and its applications to the search for axion-like particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18882)
*Tylor Adkins,Shahed Shayan Arani,Kam Arnold,Carlo Baccigalupi,Darcy R. Barron,Bryce Bixler,Yuji Chinone,Matthew R. Chu,Kevin T. Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Simons Array望远镜在90 GHz波段对蟹状星云（Tau A）的偏振角随时间变化进行了搜寻，未发现显著的全局偏振振荡信号，给出了振幅上限A < 0.12°，并据此对轴子类粒子（ALP）-光子耦合强度g_{aγγ}给出新的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tau A被广泛用作毫米波天文观测中偏振角校准源，其稳定性需验证；同时，其时间分辨偏振观测可用于探测轴子类粒子（ALPs）。

Method: 使用Simons Array在2023年观测季的90 GHz频段数据，分析Tau A偏振角的时间变异性，开展偏振振荡搜寻，并结合ALP物理模型将振荡振幅限制转化为对ALP-光子耦合常数g_{aγγ}的约束。

Result: 未在所考察频率范围内（3.39 year⁻¹ 至 1.50 day⁻¹）探测到全局偏振振荡信号，得到95%置信度下振荡振幅上限A < 0.12°；由此导出ALP-光子耦合强度上限g_{aγγ} < 3.84×10⁻¹² × (m_a/10⁻²¹ eV)，对应ALP质量范围4.4×10⁻²²–7.2×10⁻²⁰ eV；对POLARBEAR此前报道的2.5σ异常信号未予证实，但亦未在95%置信水平排除。

Conclusion: Tau A在当前观测精度下仍可作为可靠的偏振校准源；本工作为ALP参数空间提供了新的、有竞争力的实验约束，尤其在超轻质量区。

Abstract: We present a search for polarization oscillation of the Crab Nebula, also known as Tau A, at millimeter wavelengths using observations with the Simons Array, the successor experiment to POLARBEAR. We follow up on previous work by POLARBEAR using 90 GHz band data of the 2023 observing season of the Simons Array to evaluate the variability of Tau A's polarization angle. Tau A is widely used as a polarization angle calibration source in millimeter-wave astronomy, and thus it is necessary to validate the stability. Additionally, an interesting application of the time-resolved polarimetry of Tau A is to search for axion-like particles (ALPs). We do not detect a global signal across the frequencies considered in this analysis and place a median 95% upper bound of polarization oscillation amplitude $A<0.12^{\circ}$ over oscillation frequencies from 3.39 year$^{-1}$ to 1.50 day$^{-1}$. This constrains the ALP-photon coupling at a median 95% upper bound of $g_{aγγ}< 3.84\times 10^{-12}\times\left(m_a/10^{-21}\,\mathrm{eV}\right)$ in the mass range from $4.4\times10^{-22}$ to $7.2\times10^{-20}$ eV, assuming the ALP constitutes all of dark matter, its field is a stochastic Gaussian field, and it is the sole source of Tau A's polarization angle oscillation. Additionally, we do not detect signal at the frequencies where 2.5$σ$ hints were previously reported by POLARBEAR, but we do not exclude these signals at the 95% confidence level.

Plazas Malagón,A. Porredon,K. Romer,E. Sanchez,D. Sanchez Cid,I. Sevilla,M. Smith,M. Soares-Santos,E. Suchyta,M. Swanson,C. To,N. Weaverdyck,J. Weller*

TL;DR: 本文利用暗能量巡天（DES）第三年数据的弱引力透镜测量，对阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜（ACT）第五次数据释放中通过SZ效应选出的443个星系团进行质量校准，并约束其流体静力学质量偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确校准SZ效应观测到的星系团质量对利用星系团开展宇宙学和天体物理研究至关重要；当前SZ质量标度关系依赖于X射线标定并假设流体静力学平衡，存在系统性偏差（即质量偏差1−b），需用独立方法（如弱透镜）进行检验与约束。

Method: 采用分层贝叶斯模型分析堆叠弱透镜信号，结合各星系团的红移和SZ测量；系统考虑多种不确定性：弱透镜boost因子、中心偏移效应、源星系测光红移分布及剪切定标误差，并在分析中对其边缘化处理。

Result: 全样本得到质量-可观测量关系归一化精度约7%，平均WL质量M500c = 5.4×10¹⁴ M⊙；测得整体流体静力学质量偏差为1−b = 0.75⁺⁰·⁰⁴₋₀·₀₆；高低红移子样本分别为0.58⁺⁰·⁰⁶₋₀·₀₅ 和 0.82⁺⁰·⁰⁷₋₀·₀₇；引入红移和质量依赖的偏差模型后，发现1−b随红移显著下降（幂律指数−2.0⁺⁰·⁷₋₀·₄，99.95%置信），但无显著质量依赖趋势；结果对各类系统误差稳健。

Conclusion: 本工作提供了基于弱透镜的高精度ACT星系团质量校准，证实了SZ质量存在显著红移依赖的流体静力学偏差，支持非平衡或非热压成分随红移演化；该校准结果将有力支撑ACT星系团在宇宙学参数限制和星系团物理研究中的应用。

Abstract: We use weak gravitational lensing measurements from Year 3 Dark Energy Survey data to calibrate the masses of 443 galaxy clusters selected via the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect from Atacama Cosmology Telescope Data Release 5 maps of the cosmic microwave background. We incorporate redshift and SZ measurements for individual clusters into a hierarchical model for the stacked lensing signals and perform Bayesian analyses to constrain the hydrostatic mass bias of the clusters. Our treatment of systematic uncertainties includes a prescription for measuring and accounting for the weak lensing boost factor, consideration of a miscentering effect, as well as marginalization over uncertainties in the source galaxy photometric redshift distributions and shear calibration. The resultant constraints on the normalization of the mass-observable relation have a precision of approximately 7\%, with the mean WL halo mass of $M_{\rm 500c} = 5.4 \times 10^{14} M_{\odot}$. We measure the bias between the true cluster mass and the mass estimated from the SZ signal based on an X-ray--calibrated scaling relation assuming hydrostatic equilibrium, to be $1-b = 0.75^{+0.04}_{-0.06}$ over the full sample. When splitting the clusters into high ($z$=0.43-0.70) and low ($z$=0.15-0.43) redshift bins, we measure $1-b = 0.58^{+0.06}_{-0.05}$ and $0.82^{+0.07}_{-0.07}$, respectively. When introducing additional freedom in redshift and mass to the hydrostatic bias model, we find that $1-b$ decreases with redshift (with the power law of $-2.0^{+0.7}_{-0.4}$, 99.95\% confidence), consistent with findings from other recent studies, while we do not find any significant trend in mass. We also demonstrate that our result is robust against various systematics. The weak-lensing mass calibration presented in this study will be a useful tool for using the ACT clusters as probes of astrophysics and cosmology.

### [87] [$Ω_1Ω_2$-$Λ$CDM: A promising natural extension of the standard model of cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19000)
*Suresh Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种ΛCDM的自然扩展模型Ω₁Ω₂-ΛCDM，通过在(1+z)幂级数中展开宇宙总能量密度，引入两个可观测的暗能量项Ω₁(1+z)和Ω₂(1+z)²，以缓解哈勃常数H₀张力；结合Planck CMB与DESI BAO数据，发现该模型可使H₀与SH0ES测量一致（Planck单独分析得H₀=75.4⁺³·⁹₋₂·₃ km/s/Mpc），加入BAO后张力降至~2.5σ；模型具平滑的精质–幻影转变及渐近德西特行为，且不破坏早期宇宙物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缓解标准ΛCDM框架下CMB与距离阶梯观测之间存在的哈勃常数（H₀）张力问题。

Method: 构建Ω₁Ω₂-ΛCDM模型，将总能量密度按(1+z)幂级数展开，引入两个新暗能量参数Ω₁和Ω₂；联合使用Planck CMB和DESI BAO观测数据进行贝叶斯参数估计与约束。

Result: Planck单独分析给出H₀ = 75.4^{+3.9}_{-2.3} km/s/Mpc，与SH0ES结果一致；加入DESI BAO后H₀张力降至约2.5σ；模型展现出平滑的w_de从>−1到<−1的过渡，并渐近趋于−1；低红移BAO数据对该模型的约束仍较弱。

Conclusion: 受控的晚期宇宙偏离ΛCDM（如Ω₁Ω₂-ΛCDM）可有效改善宇宙学一致性，为解决H₀张力提供有物理动机的新路径，同时保持早期宇宙标准物理不变。

Abstract: We investigate a natural extension of the standard $Λ$CDM framework, the $Ω_1Ω_2$-$Λ$CDM model, in which the total energy density of the universe is expanded in powers of $1+z$. This parameterization recovers the standard $Λ$CDM scenario and introduces two additional, observationally testable contributions to the dark energy sector, $Ω_1(1+z)$ and $Ω_2(1+z)^2$, alongside the cosmological constant. Using Planck CMB and DESI BAO data, we find that this framework is suitable for relaxing the Hubble tension. The Planck CMB data alone allow substantial freedom in late-time dynamics, yielding $H_0 = 75.4^{+3.9}_{-2.3}\;\mathrm{km\;s^{-1}\;Mpc^{-1}}$, fully consistent with distance-ladder measurements from the SH0ES collaboration. When DESI BAO data are included in the analysis, the late-time expansion history becomes more tightly anchored, reducing the $H_0$ discrepancy to $\sim 2.5σ$ level. This highlights the limited constraining power of currently available low-redshift data measurements, especially in the context of the $Ω_1Ω_2$-$Λ$CDM model, where dynamical dark energy dominates the background expansion over a relatively large redshift range. The model naturally exhibits a smooth quintessence--phantom transition followed by asymptotic de Sitter behavior of the dark energy equation of state, alters late-time cosmic dynamics, and preserves standard early-universe physics. Overall, our results demonstrate that controlled late-time deviations from $Λ$CDM can improve cosmological concordance.

### [88] [DESI DR2 Constraints on the $R_h=ct$ Universe: Model Viability and Comparison with $Λ$CDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19175)
*Amritansh Mehrotra,S. K. J. Pacif,A. F. Santos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估ΛCDM与Rh=ct两种宇宙学模型对当前观测数据（如宇宙钟、Ia型超新星、BAO）的拟合能力，并探讨JWST发现高红移成熟星系所引发的宇宙年龄争议。

Method: 基于χ²统计量、AIC、BIC及贝叶斯因子进行联合统计分析；对比两模型对H(z)、q(z)演化及宇宙年龄的预测。

Result: ΛCDM在所有信息准则和似然值上均优于Rh=ct；能自然描述减速—加速转变，而Rh=ct仅给出线性膨胀；ΛCDM预言的宇宙年龄与Planck 2018一致，Rh=ct则给出更老年龄。

Conclusion: ΛCDM仍是目前数据支持更强的模型，但JWST新结果提示可能需在标准范式外寻求改进，以彻底理解宇宙演化。

Abstract: We carry out a comparative analysis of the standard $Λ$CDM cosmological model and the alternative $R_h=ct$ framework using recent observational data from cosmic chronometers, Type Ia supernova, and baryon acoustic oscillations. The study evaluates the ability of each model to reproduce the observed expansion history of the Universe through a joint statistical assessment based on the chi-squared statistics, Akaike Information Criterion (AIC), Bayesian Information Criteria (BIC), and Bayes factor. While both models yield acceptable fits, $Λ$CDM consistently attains lower information-criterion values and higher likelihood, indicating a superior overall performance. An examination of the redshift evolution of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ and the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ shows that $Λ$CDM naturally captures the transition from early-time deceleration to late-time acceleration, where as $R_h=ct$ predicts a strictly linear expansion. We also estimate the age of the Universe within both models, finding that $Λ$CDM prediction agrees with the Planck 2018 result, while the linear expansion in $R_h=ct$ leads to an older cosmic age. Recent JWST observations of unexpectedly mature high-redshift galaxies have reopened the discussion regarding whether the Universe may be older than implied by the standard model; although these results remain under active investigation, they underscore that fully resolving cosmic evolution may require refinements beyond the concordance paradigm.

Abstract: We investigate the synergy between large-scale structure (LSS) observations and gravitational wave (GW) events for testing modified gravity. We describe the considered modified gravity scenarios, the relevant LSS and GW observables, and the synthetic forecast methodology. ### [90] [Dynamics of clusters of galaxies in the presence of dark energy: Virgo cluster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19436)
*H. A. Harutyunian,E. H. Nikogosyan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统计方法来识别星系团内星系的径向运动，并以室女座星系团为例，发现其子结构中的星系比整体星系团更亮，且每个子群包含一个活动星系；子群中星系的平均星等与其平均速度呈正相关，这被解释为星系团膨胀的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于重子物质与暗能量载体之间的相互作用，所有重子物质构型都会获得能量并必然发生膨胀，这一结论适用于包括星系团在内的所有重子宇宙层级。

Method: 提出一种简单的统计方法来识别星系团内星系的径向运动，并以室女座星系团为样本分析其结构特征和子结构。

Result: 发现室女座星系团存在由不同多重性星系群组成的子结构；子结构中的星系比整个星系团更亮，且每个子群均含一个活动星系；子群中星系的平均星等与平均速度呈正相关。

Conclusion: 星系平均星等与平均速度的正相关性可作为星系团正在膨胀的观测证据，支持重子物质受暗能量影响而普遍膨胀的观点。

Abstract: It is shown that, owing to the interaction of baryonic matter with the carrier of dark energy, all configurations of baryonic matter acquire energy and inevitably must expand. This conclusion applies to all hierarchical levels of the baryonic universe, including galaxy clusters. We propose a simple statistical method for identifying possible radial motions of galaxies within clusters. To illustrate this method, we examined the structural features of the Virgo galaxy cluster and identified its substructure, comprising groups of galaxies of varying multiplicity. Galaxies in the substructure are somewhat brighter than those in the overall cluster, and each subgroup contains an active galaxy. Subgroups are considered to be the product of primordial ejections of matter from the central generator galaxy. It is shown that the average stellar magnitude of galaxies in subgroups positively correlates with their average velocity. This correlation can be interpreted as evidence of cluster expansion.

### [91] [Revealing the intricacies of radio galaxies and filaments in the merging galaxy cluster Abell 2255. II. Properties of filaments using multi-frequency radio data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19471)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深入理解Abell 2255中射电丝状结构的起源与物理性质，需高分辨率成像与宽频谱分析以区分不同宇宙线成分并约束其辐射年龄和磁场。

Method: 采用LOFAR-VLBI宽视场成像技术（144 MHz，1.5角秒分辨率，56小时观测），联合uGMRT（1260 MHz）和VLA（1520 MHz）数据，构建谱指数图、辐射年龄图、等离子体磁场图，并利用RM合成技术获取偏振信息。

Result: 发现延伸约250 kpc、谱指数α>2的新陡谱丝状结构（Trail）；丝状结构整体积分谱指数为1.1–1.7；原TRG尾部存在多组谱指数不同的重叠结构；偏振仅见于尾部及最亮丝状区，最高达22%。

Conclusion: 原TRG是驱动这些丝状结构（包括远距离部分）的主要能量源；高分辨率多频段联合分析对揭示星系团内复杂射电结构的形成机制至关重要。

Abstract: In this paper, we aim to further analyze the filaments in Abell 2255 combining LOFAR data with uGMRT (1260 MHz) and VLA (1520 MHz) data to constrain the spectral shape of the filaments. This allows studying their morphological properties, required to understand their origin, at unprecedentedly high resolution (~2.3 kpc), crucial to disentangle the different cosmic ray components that populate the Original TRG. We produced a LOFAR-VLBI map at 1.5" resolution using the wide-field technique with 56 hours of observations. This was the first time this technique was used for a galaxy cluster, especially for such deep observations. uGMRT and VLA data have been calibrated and imaged to produce spectral index maps and to apply further techniques to extract additional information, such as the radiative ages of the filaments or their equipartition magnetic field. Polarization information was also obtained using VLA through the rotation measure synthesis technique. Thanks to the LOFAR-VLBI wide-field image at 144 MHz, we revealed additional, very steep ($α> 2$) filaments beyond those attached to the radio galaxy, extending for around 250 kpc and previously known as the Trail. Combining LOFAR-VLBI with uGMRT and VLA, we found integrated spectral values between 1.1-1.7 for the filaments. Spectral analysis revealed also that the Original TRG has a complex structure, showing overlapping features with distinct spectral indices that extend throughout its tail. Polarized emission emerges only from the tail and the brightest part of the filaments, with values up to $22\%$. Although there is no clear scenario regarding the formation of filaments, we highlight the importance of the Original TRG as the main driver of such structures, even at larger distances from the core.

</details>


### [92] [Low-redshift 3D Lyman-α Forest Correlations with China Space Station Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19474)
*Ting Tan,Huanyuan Shan,Eric Armengaud*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了利用中国空间站望远镜（CSST）的紫外无狭缝光谱仪测量低红移（z < 2）莱曼-α（Lyα）森林三维相关性的前景，通过构建模拟光谱预测了Lyα自相关及与类星体（QSO）、发射线星系（ELG）交叉相关的约束能力，并首次实现z<2的Lyα三维表征和BAO测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lyα森林虽能有效示踪大尺度结构，但其在z<2的三维聚类尚未被观测；需借助新一代巡天设备（如CSST）填补该红移区间空白，并连接高红移Lyα与低红shift星系巡天。

Method: 基于CSST预期观测参数（深度、光谱分辨率、噪声）构建类星体模拟光谱，计算Lyα自相关函数及与QSO/ELG的交叉相关函数，并用各向异性红移空间聚集模型拟合以预报参数约束。

Result: 在z_eff≈1.59处，Lyα偏置参数精度达10–30%；Lyα自相关+Lyα-QSO（或Lyα-ELG）交叉相关可分别以2.5σ（3.7σ）显著性探测BAO特征，对各向同性BAO尺度约束达~10%（7%）。

Conclusion: CSST有望首次实现z<2 Lyα森林的三维表征，并提供独立的低红移Lyα基BAO测量，弥合高红移Lyα与低红移星系巡天之间的观测鸿沟。

Abstract: While the Lyman-$α$ (Ly$α$) forest traces the large-scale matter distribution over a wide range of redshift, its three-dimensional (3D) clustering at $z < 2$ has not yet been measured. We investigate the prospects for measuring low-redshift Ly$α$ correlations with the UV slitless spectroscopic instrument of the China Space Station Telescope (CSST). We construct mock CSST quasar spectra that reproduce the expected survey depth, spectral resolution and noise properties, and derive Ly$α$ auto-correlation functions and cross-correlations with quasars (QSO) and emission-line galaxies (ELG) in the range $1.1 < z < 2.0$. We then interpret these three-dimensional correlation functions with a standard anisotropic redshift-space clustering model and obtain forecast constraints on the Ly$α$ and tracer parameters. At an effective redshift $z_{\rm eff}=1.59$ (1.58 for ELGs), the Ly$α$ bias parameters will be measured with a 10-30\% precision, depending on priors on other tracer's biases. We also forecast a marginal $2.5σ$ ($3.7σ$) detection of the BAO feature, corresponding to a $\sim$10\% (7\%) constraint on the isotropic BAO scale, from the combination of Ly$α$ auto- and Ly$α$-QSO (ELG) cross-correlations. These results show that CSST can provide the first three-dimensional characterization of the low-redshift Ly$α$ forest and a complementary Ly$α$-based BAO measurement at $z < 2$, helping to link galaxy clustering surveys with high-redshift Ly$α$ forest studies.

### [93] [Do low-redshift observations open the doors to an open universe?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19565)
*Deng Wang,Olga Mena,Salvatore Capozziello,David Mota*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用DESI BAO和Ia型超新星（SN Ia）等低红移观测数据，发现宇宙空间曲率显著偏离零（即非平直），呈现约2–5σ的开放宇宙证据，与高红移Planck CMB数据暗示的闭合宇宙存在明显张力，挑战标准暴胀理论及ΛCDM模型的平坦性预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检测宇宙空间曲率是否显著偏离零对暴胀理论和基础物理具有深远意义；高红移CMB数据（如Planck）显示约2σ闭合宇宙迹象，而低红移BAO和SN Ia观测具有弱依赖早期宇宙物理、系统误差独立、距离对曲率敏感等优势，亟需用其独立检验宇宙曲率。

Method: 联合分析DESI的重子声波振荡（BAO）数据、多组Ia型超新星（SN Ia）数据（含DES Y5样本），并结合CMB给出的声学角尺度θ⋆先验，通过参数估计（如Ω_K）约束宇宙空间曲率，在不同数据组合下进行统计显著性检验。

Result: 仅用DESI BAO+SN Ia即得~2σ开放宇宙证据；加入θ⋆后显著性升至>3σ，使用DES Y5 SN数据时达5σ；该结果在更换高红移先验后依然稳健。

Conclusion: 低红移观测一致支持开放宇宙，与高红移CMB结果存在新的、显著的曲率张力，表明当前ΛCDM及其非平直扩展模型可能面临根本性挑战，提示需重新审视暴胀预言或引入新物理。

Abstract: The detection of a significant deviation from a zero curvature would have profound consequences for inflationary theories and fundamental physics. Relative to high-redshift Planck's CMB measurements, indicating a $\sim 2σ$ evidence for a closed universe, low-redshift observations of BAO and SN Ia have the advantages of weak dependence on early universe physics, independently observational systematics, and strong redshift dependence of distances in constraining the cosmic curvature. Using the integrated observations from DESI BAO and SN Ia, we find an unexpected $2σ$ evidence for an open universe, regardless of the SN Ia sample employed. When considering DESI, SN Ia and the acoustic scale $θ_\star$ data, the preference for an open universe exceeds the $3σ$ level, reaching $5σ$ for the case of DESY5 Supernovae data. Therefore, low-redshift observations favor an open universe, and this preference persists even when alternative high-redshift priors are adopted. Our results point to the existence of an additional tension between high- and low-redshift observations, present also in non-flat models beyond the minimal $Λ$CDM scheme, thereby challenging the standard inflationary predictions.

### [94] [Deep Learning for Primordial $B$-mode Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19577)
*Eric Guzman,Joel Meyers*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度学习（ResUNet-CMB）的方法，用于同时估计并去除多种次级B模偏振污染源（如引力透镜、片状再电离、宇宙偏振旋转），从而提升原初引力波振幅参数r的无偏、近似最优估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 次级B模偏振（尤其是引力透镜效应）将成为未来CMB实验中探测原初引力波的主要瓶颈；现有去透镜方法难以同时处理多种次级源且易引入非高斯统计复杂性。

Method: 利用深度学习模型ResUNet-CMB，对多源次级B模（透镜、片状再电离、偏振旋转等）进行联合建模、估计与去除，并将其嵌入似然分析框架中。

Result: 该方法能实现对原初引力波振幅r的近似最优、无偏估计，显著优于传统单源去透镜策略，在低噪声多频CMB数据中展现出鲁棒性和高精度。

Conclusion: 深度学习为协同处理多种次级B模污染提供了统一、高效且统计上严谨的新范式，有望成为下一代CMB实验提取原初引力波信号的关键技术。

Abstract: The search for primordial gravitational waves is a central goal of cosmic microwave background (CMB) surveys. Isolating the characteristic $B$-mode polarization signal sourced by primordial gravitational waves is challenging for several reasons: the amplitude of the signal is inherently small; astrophysical foregrounds produce $B$-mode polarization contaminating the signal; and secondary $B$-mode polarization fluctuations are produced via the conversion of $E$ modes. Current and future low-noise, multi-frequency observations enable sufficient precision to address the first two of these challenges such that secondary $B$ modes will become the bottleneck for improved constraints on the amplitude of primordial gravitational waves. The dominant source of secondary $B$-mode polarization is gravitational lensing by large scale structure. Various strategies have been developed to estimate the lensing deflection and to reverse its effects the CMB, thus reducing confusion from lensing $B$ modes in the search for primordial gravitational waves. However, a few complications remain. First, there may be additional sources of secondary $B$-mode polarization, for example from patchy reionization or from cosmic polarization rotation. Second, the statistics of delensed CMB maps can become complicated and non-Gaussian, especially when advanced lensing reconstruction techniques are applied. We previously demonstrated how a deep learning network, ResUNet-CMB, can provide nearly optimal simultaneous estimates of multiple sources of secondary $B$-mode polarization. In this paper, we show how deep learning can be applied to estimate and remove multiple sources of secondary $B$-mode polarization, and we further show how this technique can be used in a likelihood analysis to produce nearly optimal, unbiased estimates of the amplitude of primordial gravitational waves.

### [95] [Non-local-in-time structure formation and sixth-order galaxy bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19578)
*Alex Edison,Matthew Lewandowski,Leonardo Senatore*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文系统构建了大尺度结构有效场论中非局域时间星系偏差展开，并计算出六阶非局域时间偏差算子基共57个独立偏差，比局域时间情形多11个，表明高阶聚类统计可区分星系形成的局域与非局域时间机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为更精确描述星系形成过程中时间非局域性的影响，需扩展传统局域时间偏差模型，以捕捉星系密度对过去不同时刻暗物质场的依赖。

Method: 从星系过密的一般非局域时间表达式出发，系统推导并显式计算了空间导数领头阶下的六阶偏差算子基，同时推导了扰动核的递推关系及其多腿软极限性质。

Result: 得到57个独立的六阶非局域时间偏差算子；发现其数量超过局域时间情形（46个）；证实高阶统计量在单一红移处可敏感探测星系形成时间。

Conclusion: 非局域时间偏差展开是刻画星系形成历史的关键理论工具，高阶聚类观测有望约束星系形成的时间演化过程。

Abstract: We present a systematic construction of the non-local-in-time galaxy bias expansion in the Effective Field Theory of Large-Scale Structure. In order to fully capture time non-locality up to sixth order, we must take into account that every field can contribute non-locally from a separate time in the past. Starting from the general non-local-in-time expression for the galaxy overdensity, we explicitly compute the complete sixth-order basis of bias operators at leading order in spatial derivatives, finding 57 independent biases, compared to 46 in the corresponding local-in-time expansion. As previously found at fifth order, this difference implies that higher-order clustering statistics can distinguish between local- and non-local-in-time galaxy formation, and thus are sensitive, at a single redshift, to the formation time of galaxies. Along the way, we obtain recursion relations for the perturbative kernels and show that they satisfy specific multi-leg soft limits when the sum of a subset of the external momenta goes to zero.

### [96] [InterACTing dark radiation models after ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19633)
*William Cvetko,Melissa Joseph,Gustavo Marques-Tavares*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜DR6数据检验两类相互作用暗辐射模型（WZDR和nuADaM）对哈勃张力的缓解能力，发现高ℓ数据显著收紧参数限制，大幅压缩此前允许较高H₀值的参数空间，表明ACT DR6严重限制了相互作用暗辐射作为哈勃张力解决方案的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决哈勃常数（H₀）在早期宇宙（CMB）与局域距离阶梯测量之间的显著张力，此前基于Planck数据的两类相互作用暗辐射模型（WZDR和nuADaM）可有效缓解该张力。

Method: 将ACT DR6高精度、高ℓ角功率谱数据（深入阻尼尾区）纳入贝叶斯参数估计框架，分别对WZDR、nuADaM及一个包含自由传播与自相互作用暗辐射的广义模型进行约束分析，并与Planck结果对比。

Result: ACT DR6数据使两类模型中额外辐射成分的约束显著收紧，几乎完全排除了此前支持较高H₀值的参数区域；广义模型在纯自由传播和纯自相互作用极限下，其约束与ACT单独分析结果一致。

Conclusion: ACT DR6观测强烈削弱了相互作用暗辐射模型缓解哈勃张力的能力，表明该类模型作为张力解决方案已受到严峻挑战。

Abstract: In this work we assess the implications of the Atacama Cosmology Telescope DR6 measurements for two interacting dark radiation scenarios previously shown to mitigate the Hubble tension. The first model, Wess-Zumino dark radiation (WZDR), features a mass threshold in the dark sector that induces a step-like reduction in the dark radiation abundance as the dark temperature evolves. The second model, new atomic dark matter (nuADaM), introduces dark radiation that remains coupled to a subcomponent of dark matter until shortly before matter-radiation equality. Earlier analyses using Planck data demonstrated that these interactions significantly relax constraints on the dark radiation density and allow values of $H_0$ consistent with local distance-ladder determinations. Incorporating ACT DR6, which extends CMB measurements deep into the high-$\ell$ damping tail, we find that constraints on the additional radiation component tighten substantially in both scenarios, closing most of the parameter space that previously enabled higher values of $H_0$. We further analyze a generalized model including both free-streaming and self-interacting dark radiation, and show that the resulting constraints are consistent with ACT's findings for the limiting cases of purely free-streaming or purely self-interacting radiation. Overall, ACT DR6 significantly restricts interacting dark radiation as a solution to the Hubble tension.

### [97] [A cosmologist's take on Little Red Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19666)
*Valerio De Luca,Loris Del Grosso,Gabriele Franciolini,Konstantinos Kritos,Emanuele Berti,Daniel D'Orazio,Joseph Silk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LRDs中黑洞质量远超其恒星质量，挑战标准星系演化模型，亟需解释其极端质量比的起源，尤其是是否源于原初黑洞（PBH）。

Method: 结合CMB μ-畸变限制排除直接PBH形成；模拟轻质量PBH通过层级并合增长；数值模拟气体吸积（联合追踪金属丰度演化）；以QSO1为极端案例约束参数空间。

Result: 直接形成被CMB限制排除；层级并合受限于高红移暗晕稀缺性；吸积模型在特定参数下可解释LRDs观测性质，QSO1的极低金属丰度和高质量对模型构成强约束。

Conclusion: LRDs中的超大质量黑洞更可能通过原初黑洞吸积气体而非直接形成或并合形成；金属丰度演化是区分形成通道的关键诊断指标。

Abstract: The James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) has uncovered a population of compact, high-redshift sources, the Little Red Dots (LRDs), which may host supermassive black holes (BHs) significantly heavier than their stellar content compared with local scaling relations. These objects challenge standard models of early galaxy formation and may represent an extreme class of early BH hosts. In this paper, we investigate whether these BHs could have a primordial origin. We first show that the direct formation of these BH masses in the early Universe is excluded by stringent CMB $μ$-distortion limits. We then investigate the assembly of massive BHs from lighter, observationally allowed primordial black holes (PBHs) via hierarchical mergers, finding that, although this channel can operate depending on the merger history, it faces challenges in explaining the observations due to the rarity of the required high-redshift dark matter halos. Finally, we estimate gas accretion onto intermediate-mass PBHs, while jointly tracking metallicity evolution, and identify regions of parameter space in which such growth could reproduce the observed properties of LRDs. As a special case, we focus on the strongly lensed source QSO1, whose extremely low metallicity and large mass provide a stringent test of these formation channels.

### [98] [Are Primordial Black Holes Truly Fine-Tuned?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19668)
*A. J. Iovino,A. Riotto*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文质疑了单场暴胀模型中产生原初黑洞所需参数微调程度的传统定义，提出采用Wilson自然性准则来重新评估其自然性，并证明这些模型在技术上并非不自然。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上对原初黑洞产生模型的微调批评存在缺陷：当原初黑洞丰度越小、宇宙学上越无害时，反而被判定为越需微调；而一个可靠的微调度量应在真正需要精细调节时给出大值，在典型敏感情形下接近1。

Method: 采用（修正版）Wilson自然性准则作为量化微调和自然性的工具，重新分析单场暴胀模型中通过曲率扰动功率谱小尺度增强产生原初黑洞的情形。

Result: 基于Wilson自然性准则的分析表明，这类原初黑洞产生模型并不具备技术上的不自然性。

Conclusion: 原初黑洞生成模型不应因其传统意义上的‘高微调’而被轻易否定；使用更合理的自然性判据后，其理论可行性得到支持。

Abstract: Single-field inflationary models which generate primordial black holes through the enhancement of the curvature primordial power at small scales are commonly criticized and frequently dismissed because they require a large amount of fine-tuning in the parameters setting the ultra slow-roll phase. However, the standarly adopted definition of fine-tuning has a clear drawback: the more the primordial black hole abundance is small and cosmologically harmless, the larger the parameter space is fine-tuned. A reliable measure of fine-tuning should deliver a large value when the primordial black hole abundance is fine-tuned and at the same time reduce to something close to unity when it encounters typical sensitivity. Motivated by such arguments, we use the (modified version of) Wilson's naturalness criterion for quantifying the fine-tuning and naturalness and we show that the primordial black hole models are not technically unnatural.

### [99] [CoBiTS: Single-detector discrimination of binary black hole signals from glitches using deep learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17975)
*Matthew VanDyke,Kexuan Wu,Sukanta Bose*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Conformer架构的二值化神经网络CoBiTS，用于在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA探测器数据中区分双黑洞引力波信号与非高斯、非平稳噪声（如glitches），显著提升了高质比信号与典型噪声的鉴别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波搜索中，大量噪声‘glitches’会误触发双黑洞模板，产生需人工复核的候选事件，亟需自动、鲁棒的分类方法。

Method: 提出CoBiTS模型：以单探测器应变时间序列片段为输入，采用Conformer架构（融合卷积层与Transformer自注意力机制）建模时序特征，输出该片段属于双黑洞信号或glitch的显著性得分。

Result: CoBiTS在区分高质比双黑洞信号与blips、散射光等glitches方面表现优异，即使信号与glitch并发或重叠也能保持高判别性能。

Conclusion: Conformer架构能有效结合局部特征提取与长程依赖建模能力，使CoBiTS成为当前引力波数据中强噪声背景下信号识别的有力工具。

Abstract: We develop a Conformer neural network, called Conformer Binary neTwork Search, or CoBiTS, for distinguishing binary black hole (BBH) gravitational wave (GW) signals from non-Gaussian and non-stationary noise artifacts in the data from current generation LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors. A large subset of these transient noise artifacts, termed as ``glitches'' for short, trigger BBH search templates. Some of them go on to produce detection candidates and require human vetting, supported by data quality tools, to be correctly identified and vetoed. In its current version, CoBiTS takes as inputs single-detector strain timeseries snippets, claimed by other search pipelines to be containing GW candidates, and outputs the significance of each snippet to contain a BBH signal and a glitch. CoBiTS is shown to be particularly effective in discriminating high-mass BBH signals from blips and scattered light glitches, even when a signal is near concurrent or overlapping with a glitch. The performance of CoBiTS gains from employing Conformer, which is a specialized model that combines convolutional layers and Transformer architecture for sequence modeling tasks. Conformer is especially good at leveraging the strengths of both convolutional layers -- for local feature extraction -- and self-attention layers -- for capturing long-range dependencies.

### [100] [Bridging stellar evolution and planet formation: from birth, to survivors of the fittest, to the second generation of planets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17976)

To take full advantage of these developments by the 2040s, we should develop the capabilities required to image the varied dusty environments in which planets are entrained over their lifetime. ### [102] [Characterization of telecentric dual-etalon Fabry-Pérot systems from observational data. Properties of the CRISP2 instrument at the Swedish 1-m Solar Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18039)
*J. de la Cruz Rodríguez,G. B. Scharmer,P. Sütterlin,J. Leenaarts,M. G. Löfdahl,D. Kiselman,T. Hillberg,O. Andriienko*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需改变光学配置或外部光源即可表征双标准具成像法布里-珀罗干涉仪（FPI）空间参数变化的方法，重点应用于太阳观测仪器CRISP2，通过前向建模与宁静太阳光谱模板拟合观测数据，精确获取腔长分离、标准具反射率及前置滤光片的空间变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 成像FPI观测在太阳物理中被广泛用于推断光球层和色球层的物理参数，但其建模精度高度依赖对仪器谱线轮廓（SIP）的准确刻画；而现有方法常需额外校准设备或改变光路，缺乏适用于常规观测的非侵入式表征手段。

Method: 构建包含双标准具腔长分离、反射率及前置滤光片空间变化的FPI前向退化模型，并结合盘心平均宁静太阳光谱模板，拟合两组实测数据；评估不同传输谱函数形式的影响，特别考察次级透射峰（±1自由光谱范围）与前置滤光曲线建模精度对反射率反演的作用。

Result: CRISP2双标准具腔长在全视场内极为平坦（RMS变化<1.9 nm）；617.3 nm处主、次标准具反射率RMS变化分别为0.4%和0.3%；证实在窄带前置滤光条件下可放宽对次级透射峰建模的要求，但一般情形下必须包含±1 FSR透射峰并精细估计前置滤光曲线才能准确反演反射率。

Conclusion: 所提方法为telecentric配置下的双标准具FPI提供了实用、非侵入式的全场参数标定方案，显著提升了基于FPI观测的太阳大气参数反演精度，尤其明确了前置滤光特性与次级透射峰建模对反射率定标的关键影响。

Abstract: Imaging Fabry-Pérot Interferometer (FPI) observations are commonly used in solar physics to infer physical parameters in the photosphere and chromosphere through modeling of the observations. Such techniques require detailed knowledge of the spectral instrumental profile in order to produce accurate results. We present a method to characterize the spatial variation of parameters of dual-etalon FPI instruments mounted in telecentric configuration: spatially-resolved cavity separation and reflectivities of both etalons, and the prefilter variation across the field-of-view. We aim at characterizing the field-of-view dependence of the parameters of the new CRISP2 FPI. We have implemented a forward model of the FPI instrumental degradation combined with a template average quiet-Sun spectra at disk center in order to model two sets of observational data. Our method does not require any change in the optical setup or the utilization of external sources of illumination. We assess the validity of several functional forms in the calculation of the FPI transmission profiles. Our results show that (generally) the inclusion of the secondary transmission peaks at 1 times the Free Spectral Range and a detailed estimate of the prefilter curve is necessary to obtain accurate values of both etalon reflectivities. For narrow prefilters (relative to the FSR), the former requirement can be relaxed. Our results show that the cavity separation of CRISP2 is very flat, showing an RMS variation below 1.9 nm over the entire field-of-view for both etalons. Reflectivity RMS variations are 0.4% and 0.3% for the primary and secondary etalons at 617.3 nm. We have assessed data and modeling requirements in order to derive accurate FPI parameters and minimize errors in the determination of etalon reflectivities.

### [104] [The Impact of the MAST Data Archive](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18101)
*Richard A. Shaw,Jenny L. Novacescu,Sarah Weissman,Travis A. Berger,Clara E. Brasseur,Jeff Chamblee,Brian Cherinka,Zachary R. Claytor,Theresa Dower,Chinwe Edeani,Scott W. Fleming,Jonathan R. TL;DR: 本文分析了MAST档案中超过20个NASA空间望远镜任务的数据使用情况，统计了37,000多篇引用MAST数据的同行评议论文，发现其科学产出高、影响持久；HST和JWST的存档研究已超越原团队发表，且小/大时间分配项目单位时间产出更高；论文还探讨了引文指标在跨任务比较中的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建各任务文献数据库（涵盖近40种专业期刊），统计引用MAST数据的论文数量、发表时间、引用量及作者类型（原团队 vs. 档案用户），并分析HST与JWST的详细出版模式与时间分布。

Result: 识别出超37,000篇MAST相关 refereed 论文；多数任务在服役期及之后多年保持高产与高被引；HST档案论文数已是原团队论文的3倍以上；JWST早期迹象显示类似趋势；小/大观测时长项目单位时间产出更高；HST半数项目1.5年内首篇论文发表。

Conclusion: MAST数据具有极高的长期科研价值与广泛影响力；单纯依赖发表量或引用量衡量科学影响存在局限，需结合任务特性谨慎解读指标。

Abstract: The Barbara A. Mikulski Archive for Space Telescopes (MAST) hosts science-ready data products from over twenty NASA missions, plus community-contributed data collections, and other select surveys. The data support forefront research in the ultraviolet, optical, and near-infrared wavelength bands. We have constructed bibliographies for each mission from publications in nearly 40 professional journals, and have identified more than 37,000 refereed articles where investigators made a science usage of data hosted in MAST. The publication rate over the last 50 years shows that most MAST missions have had very high productivity during their in-service lifetimes, and have remained so for years or decades afterward. Annual citations to these publications, a measure of impact on research, are robust for most missions, with citations that grow over more than a decade. Most of the citations come from about 10% of articles within each mission.
  We examined the bibliographies of the active missions HST and JWST in greater detail. For HST the rate of archival publications exceeded those authored by the original observing teams within a decade of launch, and is now more than 3 times higher. Early indications hint that JWST archival articles could dominate the publication rate even sooner. The production of articles resulting from any given observing program can extend for decades. Programs with small and very large allocations of observing time tend to be particularly productive per unit of observing time. For HST in general, a first publication appears within 1.5 yr for 50% of observing programs, and within 3.8 yr for 80% of programs. We discuss various external factors that affect publication metrics, their strengths and limitations for measuring scientific impact, and the challenges of making meaningful comparisons of publication metrics across missions.

### [105] [Continuous Wide-Field Optical Monitoring for Very Early-Phase Transient Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18157)

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种连续宽视场光学监测的新范式，以弥补传统巡天在时间分辨率上的不足，从而捕捉瞬变天体物理事件（如超新星、千新星、伽马暴等）的最早期阶段，实现多信使（电磁波、引力波、中微子、高能粒子）协同研究，并拓展至行星防御、系外行星、变星等多个领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出并倡导基于连续宽视场光学监测的新观测范式，作为对现有警报触发式后随观测的补充甚至反向驱动（即光学发现触发更灵敏的引力波/中微子搜寻）。

Result: 该方法将显著提升多信使天文学能力，尤其在爱因斯坦望远镜时代实现GW事件光学对应体的快速定位与物理理解；同时为行星防御、空间碎片追踪、变星、系外行星凌星、吸积活动等提供即时科学价值。

Conclusion: 连续时域天文观测并非取代经典巡天，而是通过补全缺失的时间维度来完善其能力；后续观测由此可始于物理爆发起点，而非演化中途，从而推动真正意料之外的新发现。

Abstract: The study of transient phenomena in a multimessenger context is expected to remain a major pillar of astrophysical discovery in the decades ahead. Supernovae, Kilonovae, Black-Hole formation, Novae, GRBs, and tidal disruption events are prime examples, as their earliest phases link electromagnetic radiation to gravitational waves, neutrinos, and high-energy emission. Yet, the physics connecting these messengers unfolds within minutes to hours, while traditional surveys revisit the same region of the sky on the scale of days/weeks, missing when the event begins. Current survey facilities excel at answering what happened and how often, but essentially fail in addressing how it happened and how it couples to gravitational waves, neutrinos, or high-energy emission. Continuous wide-area optical monitoring, as proposed here, removes this limitation. The traditional approach, where a GW or neutrino alert triggers electromagnetic follow-up, is now complemented, and sometimes reversed: early electromagnetic discoveries can prompt searches for weaker gravitational waves or neutrino signals that would otherwise be missed. In the Einstein Telescope era, wide-field optical monitoring will allow us to find the optical counterparts of gravitational-wave events and understand their physics. At the same time, a telescope capable of continuous monitoring provides immediate scientific value for planetary defense, space-debris tracking, stellar variability, exoplanets transit monitoring, accretion-driven activity, and when we step into a new observational territory, the true discoveries are often the ones we did not expect. In this vision, continuous time-domain astronomy does not replace classical surveys: it completes them by supplying the missing temporal dimension. Follow-up observations remain essential, but they now begin at the physical onset of the event rather than after its evolution is underway.

### [106] [Red noise-based false alarm thresholds for astrophysical periodograms via Whittle's approximation to the likelihood](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18205)
*Amna Ejaz,Sarah Dodson-Robinson,Charlotte Haley*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于预白化（prewhitening）和Whittle近似负对数似然（NLL）的新型方法，用于在存在红噪声的天文时序数据（如径向速度、光变曲线）中计算频率依赖的虚假报警水平（FAL），显著提升周期信号（如恒星自转、系外行星）检测的统计可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Lomb-Scargle周期图常假设白噪声并据此估计虚假报警水平（FAL），但实际天文时序（如RV、光变）普遍存在红噪声，导致白噪声FAL过度敏感、产生大量假阳性；亟需一种能准确建模红噪声并据此计算稳健FAL的方法。

Method: 提出基于预白化的FAL计算方法：首先用幂律或一阶自回归（AR1）模型拟合Lomb-Scargle周期图的对数功率谱，通过最小化Whittle近似负对数似然（NLL）确定最优模型；再基于该红噪声模型功率谱计算频率依赖的FAL；该方法首次将Whittle NLL推广至非均匀采样数据。

Result: 在α Cen B、GJ 581、HD 192310实测RV数据、RV拟合挑战赛合成数据及Kepler差分自转体光变数据上验证：红噪声FAL能特异性识别真实旋转信号，而白噪声FAL在低频区误报严重；即使注入信号功率仅为主导旋转信号的8.9%，其仍超过1%红噪声FAL；HD 192310周期图中差分旋转与行星信号可直接在5%红噪声FAL下检出，无需迭代建模与减除。

Conclusion: 所提红噪声FAL方法比传统白噪声FAL更稳健、物理更合理，能有效抑制低频伪峰、提升真实周期信号（尤其弱信号）的检测置信度，适用于各类不均匀采样的天文时序分析，并已开源实现。

Abstract: Astronomers who search for periodic signals using Lomb-Scargle periodograms rely on false alarm level (FAL) estimates to identify statistically significant peaks. Although FALs are often calculated from white noise models, many astronomical time series suffer from red noise. Prewhitening is a statistical technique in which a continuum model is subtracted from log power spectrum estimate, after which the observer can proceed with a white-noise treatment. Here we present a prewhitening-based method of calculating frequency-dependent FALs. We fit power laws and autoregressive models of order 1 to each Lomb-Scargle periodogram by minimizing the Whittle approximation to the negative log-likelihood (NLL), then calculate FALs based on the best-fit model power spectrum. Our technique is a novel extension of the Whittle NLL to datasets with uneven time sampling. We demonstrate FAL calculations using observations of $α$~Cen~B, GJ~581, HD 192310, synthetic data from the radial velocity (RV) Fitting Challenge, and {\it Kepler} observations of a differential rotator. The {\it Kepler} data analysis shows that only true rotation signals are detected by red-noise FALs, while white-noise FALs suggest all spurious peaks in the low-frequency range are significant. A high-frequency sinusoid injected into $α$~Cen~B $\log R^{\prime}_{HK}$ observations exceeds the 1\% red-noise FAL despite having only 8.9\% of the power of the dominant rotation signal. In a periodogram of HD 192310 RVs, peaks associated with differential rotation and planets are detected against the 5\% red-noise FAL without iterative model fitting or subtraction. Software for calculating red noise-based FALs is available on GitHub.

</details>


### [107] [Unlocking the physics of dwarf galaxies in the 2040s: The case for a next-generation wide-field spectroscopic facility with fibres and IFUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18260)
*Crescenzo Tortora,Daniela Carollo,Leslie Hunt,Francine Marleau,Rossella Ragusa,Teymoor Saifollahi,Fernando Buitrago,Michele Cantiello,Christopher Conselice,Francesco De Paolis,Sven De Rijcke,Pierre-Alain Duc,Anna Gallazzi,Pavel E. Napolitano,Lucia Pozzetti,Justin Read,Marina Rejkuba,Joanna Sakowska,Paolo Salucci,Elham Saremi,Diana Scognamiglio,Francesco Shankar,Marilena Spavone,the Euclid Local Universe SWG*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出建设一个专用的大口径（≥20米）、大视场、高复用率光谱观测设施，配备可部署或整体式积分视场单元（IFU），以高效获取低面亮度矮星系的高质量光谱，从而深入研究暗物质分布、重子反馈、潮汐作用等关键问题，并检验ΛCDM及其他暗物质模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矮星系是宇宙中数量最多的星系，对理解暗物质、重子反馈和星系形成至关重要；但目前及计划中的设备难以高效地对银河系外矮星系进行大范围、高信噪比光谱观测，导致其动力学、恒星种群、化学增丰及暗物质含量等基本问题尚未解决。

Method: 提出设计并建造一个具备大口径（≥20米）、宽视场、高复用率、配备可部署或整体式积分视场单元（IFU）的专用光谱巡天设施，实现I_E ≳ 22–23 mag低面亮度目标的高信噪比光谱观测。

Result: 该设施将实现对红移z ∼ 1.5以内低质量星系的光谱探测，推动暗物质核结构、重子反馈、环境效应等研究，为ΛCDM及替代理论提供决定性检验，并支撑未来十年成像巡天数据的深度挖掘。

Conclusion: 建设此类专用光谱设施是当前矮星系与星系演化研究的关键突破口，不仅深化对矮星系物理的理解，还将广泛惠及强/弱引力透镜、宇宙学及整体星系演化研究。

Abstract: Dwarf galaxies ($M_{\star} \lesssim 10^{9} M_{\odot}$) are the most numerous galaxies in the Universe and critical probes of dark matter, baryonic feedback, and galaxy formation. Despite significant progress from wide-field imaging surveys, the majority of dwarf candidates beyond the Local Group will lack spectroscopic follow-up, leaving fundamental questions about their internal kinematics, stellar populations, chemical enrichment, and dark matter content unresolved. Existing and planned facilities cannot efficiently provide the necessary spectroscopy for low-surface-brightness dwarfs over wide areas. We advocate for a dedicated large-aperture ($\geq 20$ m), wide-field, highly multiplexed spectroscopic facility with deployable or monolithic IFUs, capable of high signal-to-noise observations down to $I_{\rm E} \gtrsim 22-23$ mag. Such a facility would enable transformative studies of dark matter cores, baryonic feedback, tidal interactions, environmental effects, and stellar populations, extending the spectroscopic exploration of low-mass galaxies to $z \sim 1.5$, and providing decisive tests of $Λ$CDM and alternative dark matter models. Beyond dwarfs, this capability would impact galaxy evolution, strong and weak lensing studies, and cosmology, ensuring that imaging data from the 2030s and 2040s can be fully exploited.

### [108] [Robust and scalable simulation-based inference for gravitational wave signals with gaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18290)
*Ruiting Mao,Jeong Eun Lee,Matthew C. Edwards*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于模拟的推理（SBI）框架，利用Flow Matching Posterior Estimation（FMPE）和双路径摘要器（时域1D CNN + 波let域2D CNN），直接从含间隙的LISA时序数据中稳健估计参数，显著优于传统两阶段重建与常规归一化流方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA数据流不可避免存在因维护和环境干扰导致的间隙，引发非平稳性和频谱泄漏，损害标准频域似然评估的可靠性。

Method: 提出可扩展的Simulation-Based Inference（SBI）框架，采用条件化Flow Matching Posterior Estimation（FMPE），并设计双路径摘要器：1D CNN处理时域数据以保证精度，新型基于小波的2D CNN（含非对称、膨胀卷积核）提升长时序数据的可扩展性；整体通过端到端联合训练优化。

Result: 在模拟银河系双星信号上验证，所提联合训练方法相比两阶段重建流程获得更紧致且无偏的后验分布；首次系统表明FMPE在严重数据伪影下比传统归一化流具有更优稳定性与覆盖校准性能。

Conclusion: 该SBI框架为处理带间隙的长时序引力波数据提供了鲁棒、高效、可扩展的参数估计新范式，尤其适用于LISA等空间引力波探测任务。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) data stream will inevitably contain gaps due to maintenance and environmental disturbances, introducing nonstationarities and spectral leakage that compromise standard frequency-domain likelihood evaluations. We present a scalable Simulation-Based Inference (SBI) framework capable of robust parameter estimation directly from gapped time-series data. We employ Flow Matching Posterior Estimation (FMPE) conditioned on a learned summary of the data, optimized through an end-to-end training strategy. To address the computational challenges of long-duration signals, we propose a dual-pathway summarizer architecture: a 1D Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) operating on the time domain for high precision, and a novel wavelet-based 2D CNN utilizing asymmetric, dilated kernels to achieve scalability for datasets spanning months. We demonstrate the efficacy of this framework on simulated Galactic Binary-like signals, showing that our joint training approach yields tighter, unbiased posteriors compared to two-stage reconstruction pipelines. Furthermore, we provide the first systematic comparison showing that FMPE offers superior stability and coverage calibration over conventional Normalizing Flows in the presence of severe data artifacts.

### [109] [Standard Sirens in 2040s: Probing the Cosmic Expansion History with Gravitational Waves and Spectroscopic Galaxy Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18369)
*Nicola Borghi,Michele Moresco,Richard I. Anderson,Carmelita Carbone,Andrea Cimatti,Stephanie Escoffier,Carlo Giocoli,Sean MacBride,Fatemeh Zahra Majidi,Dinko Milaković,Lauro Moscardini,Lucia Pozzetti,Margherita Talia,Elena Tomasetti*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文讨论了引力波作为标准汽笛在宇宙学中的应用，强调了获取精确红移信息对提高宇宙学参数测量精度的重要性，并指出宽视场高复用光谱设施将是2040年代引力波宇宙学的关键基础设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波提供了一种独立于传统宇宙距离阶梯的自校准光度距离测量方法，但要将其转化为宇宙学参数，必须获得红移信息。

Method: 通过识别引力波事件的电磁对应体（亮汽笛）或统计关联引力波定位体积内的潜在宿主星系（暗汽笛）来获取红移信息，并比较光谱与测光红移精度对宇宙学约束的影响。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) from compact binary coalescences have matured into a robust cosmological probe, providing self-calibrated luminosity distance measurements independent of any cosmic distance ladder, hence the term "standard sirens". The binary neutron star merger GW170817 delivered the first such measurement of the Hubble constant, demonstrating that GWs offer a path to precision cosmology with systematics orthogonal to standard cosmological probes. To convert GW distances into cosmological parameters, redshift information is essential. To maximize the scientific potential, the redshift must be obtained from individual galaxies, either by identifying electromagnetic counterparts of GW events (bright sirens) or by statistically associating potential hosts within the GW localization volume (dark sirens). The precision of these redshifts sets the achievable accuracy. Forecasts show that photometric uncertainties degrade cosmological constraints by up to an order of magnitude compared to spectroscopic ones. Wide-field, high-multiplex spectroscopic facilities will therefore be an essential infrastructure for GW cosmology in the 2040s.

SPACE brings together scientists, code developers, HPC experts, hardware (HW) manufacturers, and SW developers. This collaboration enhances exascale A&C applications, promoting the use of exascale and post-exascale computing capabilities. Additionally, SPACE addresses high-performance data analysis for the massive data outputs from exascale simulations and modern observations, using machine learning (ML) and visualisation tools. The project facilitates application deployment across platforms by focusing on code repositories and data sharing, integrating European astrophysical communities around exascale computing with standardised SW and data protocols.

### [112] [The Simons Observatory: Detector Polarization Angle Calibration using Sparse Wire Grid with Initial Data Sets of the Small Aperture Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19102)
*Hironobu Nakata,Shunsuke Adachi,Kyohei Yamada,Michael Randall,Yutaro Kasai,Kam Arnold,Bryce Bixler,Yuji Chinone,Kevin T. Crowley,Nadia Dachlythra,Samuel Day-Weiss,Nicholas Galitzki,Serena Giardiello,Bradley R. Johnson,Brian Keating,Brian J. TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种用于Simons Observatory小口径望远镜的远程可控偏振角校准系统，采用‘稀疏金属丝栅’产生可旋转线偏振信号，实现对探测器在天球上偏振方向的高精度标定，以抑制E模向B模泄漏，满足σ(r)=0.003的科学目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确校准探测器在天球上的偏振角对提高宇宙微波背景B模测量精度至关重要；偏振角标定误差会导致E模泄漏到B模中，从而影响原初引力波信号的探测。

Method: 设计并部署了一套基于稀疏金属丝栅的远程可控校准系统，可在焦平面上注入可旋转线偏振信号；开发了完整的探测器偏振角标定数据处理流程，并利用93 GHz和145 GHz实测数据进行验证。

Result: 93 GHz和145 GHz频段下相对标定统计不确定度分别为0.02°和0.03°，硬件阶段评估的系统误差为0.08°，总误差（平方和开方）小于0.1°，满足项目要求。

Conclusion: 该校准系统已在智利阿塔卡马沙漠观测站成功运行，其精度达标，为Simons Observatory实现高精度CMB B模探测提供了可靠保障。

Abstract: Improved measurements of $B$-modes in the cosmic microwave background can be obtained through accurate calibration of the orientation of detector antennas as projected onto the sky. Miscalibration of the detector polarization angle leads to a leakage of $E$-modes into $B$-modes, which can bias the detection of the latter. To achieve a $σ(r)$ of 0.003, the Simons Observatory Small Aperture Telescopes are required to calibrate the global polarization angle on the sky with an accuracy ${\lesssim}0.1^\circ$. We demonstrate a fully remote-controllable calibration system using a ``sparse wire grid," which injects a rotatable linear polarized signal across the telescope's focal plane. This calibration system is installed and operational on a Small Aperture Telescope at its observing site at the Parque Astronómico in the Atacama desert in Chile. We developed a pipeline for the detector polarization angle calibration, and demonstrate it using initial data for 93~GHz and 145~GHz frequency bands. The observed distribution of detector polarization angles is in agreement with the instrument design. Statistical uncertainties for the relatively calibrated polarization angles are $0.02^\circ$ and $0.03^\circ$ at 93~GHz and 145~GHz, respectively. Systematic uncertainty was evaluated to be $0.08^\circ$ at the hardware development and fabrication stage. Their sum in quadrature is less than $0.1^\circ$.

### [113] [Towards DM-free search for Fast Radio Bursts with Machine Learning -- I. An implementation on multibeam data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19249)
*Yao Chen,Rui Luo,Chen Wang,Yong-Kun Zhang,Shiqian Zhao,Chengbing Lyu,ZePeng Zheng,Hai Lei,DeJiang Zhou,Chenhui Niu,JinLin Han,George Hobbs,Di Li,Chengwei Liang,Siyi Tan,Ting Tian*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用EfficientNet深度学习模型，在多波束接收机数据环境下直接学习FRB时频特征，跳过显式消色散步骤；系统评估单/多波束下RFI影响，并在FAST真实巡天数据上进行验证。

Result: 模型在测试中准确率与精确率均超92%；相比TransientX和presto等传统软件显著提升搜索效率；在多波束场景下ML天然具备RFI抑制能力；在FAST实测数据中成功验证有效性。

Conclusion: 该ML驱动的免消色散方法为FRB实时、高通量搜寻提供了高效、鲁棒且可工程化落地的新范式，尤其适用于FAST等新一代大视场射电望远镜。

Abstract: Searching for fleeting radio transients like fast radio bursts (FRBs) with wide-field radio telescopes has become a common challenge in data-intensive science. Conventional algorithms normally cost enormous time to seek candidates by finding the correct dispersion measures, of which the process is so-called dedispersion. Here we present a novel scheme to identify FRB signals from raw data without dedispersion using Machine Learning (ML). Under the data environment for multibeam receivers, we train the EfficientNet model and achieve both exceeding 92% accuracy and precision in FRB recognition. We find that the searching efficiency can be significantly enhanced without the procedure of dedispersion compared with conventional softwares like TransientX and presto. Specifically, the impact of radio frequency interference (RFI) for single-beam and multibeam data has been investigated, and we find ML can naturally mitigate RFI under the multibeam environment. Finally, we validate the trained model on actual data from the current FRB surveys carried out by the Five-hundred-meter Aperture Spherical radio Telescope, which provides considerable potential for real implementation in the future.

### [115] [GALATEA: The 15-m Galactic Archaeology Spectroscopic Surveyor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.19444)
*Borja Anguiano,David Valls-Gabaud,Andrés del Pino,Guillaume F. Thomas,Alberto M. Martínez-García,Ivan Minchev,Patricia Sanchez-Blazquez,Danny Horta*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: GALATEA 是一个拟建的北半球15米口径、大视场（约1 deg²）、万光纤光谱巡天设施，旨在实现银河系及本星系群中大样本恒星的深度化学丰度与精确视向速度测量，填补现有巡天能力空白，并与30–40米极大望远镜形成互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有北半球多目标光谱巡天设施（如BOSS、APOGEE、DESI等）在视场、口径和光纤数上受限，难以对银河系外围、晕结构及本星系群邻近星系（如M31、M33及其矮卫星）开展大规模、高精度的化学动力学研究；Gaia等天测数据亟需配套的大样本光谱支持以释放6D相空间与化学信息潜力。

Method: 提出GALATEA概念设计：15米专用望远镜，配备约10,000根光纤、~1 deg²校正视场，支持中（R≈5,000–10,000）与高（R≈20,000–25,000）分辨率光谱模式，协同Gaia及未来GaiaNIR的天测与测光数据。

Result: 预计相比现有设施实现约一个数量级的巡天能力提升（∝ D² × N_fibres），首次实现对银河系外盘、翘曲、晕子结构及本星系群星系中数十万至百万量级恒星的化学丰度与视向速度联合测量。

Conclusion: GALATEA将开辟银河考古学与本星系群天体物理学的新观测前沿，成为连接大视场巡天与极大望远镜高分辨后随观测的关键枢纽设施。

Abstract: \textsc{GALATEA} (the \emph{Galactic Archaeology and Local-group Astrophysics Telescope for Extended Areas}) is a concept for a dedicated 15-m, wide-field, 10,000-fibre spectroscopic survey facility in the northern hemisphere, optimized for degree-scale, multi-object spectroscopy. With a $\sim 1~\mathrm{deg}^2$ corrected field-of-view and both medium- ($R \simeq 5{,}000$--$10{,}000$) and high-resolution ($R \simeq 20{,}000$--$25{,}000$) modes, \textsc{GALATEA} would open a new regime in Galactic and Local Group astronomy: deep, chemically detailed spectroscopy of vast samples of individual stars in the outer disc, warp, flare, halo substructures, M31, M33 and their dwarf satellites, far beyond the reach of current surveys. By delivering precise radial velocities and detailed chemical abundances for stars with exquisite astrometry and photometry from \emph{Gaia} and its proposed near-infrared successor \emph{GaiaNIR}, \textsc{GALATEA} will complete and fully exploit the 6D phase-space and chemodynamical information for these populations. Compared to existing northern multi-object spectroscopic facilities (BOSS, APOGEE, DESI, LAMOST, WEAVE, PFS), \textsc{GALATEA} delivers an order-of-magnitude jump in survey power ($\propto D^{2} \times N_{\mathrm{fibres}}$) by combining a 15-m aperture, $\sim 1~\mathrm{deg}^2$ field, and 10{,}000 fibres in a single dedicated facility. It is also strongly complementary to 30--40\,m ELTs: GALATEA provides the wide-field, high-multiplex discovery and chemodynamical mapping, while ELTs deliver deep, high-resolution follow-up of the faintest or most complex targets.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.GA'></div>

### [116] [A Correlation Between Black Hole Mass and Dark Matter Halo Concentration in Cosmological Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17964)
*John K. Nino*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文在宇宙学流体动力学模拟中发现，超大质量黑洞质量与暗物质晕浓度之间存在正相关性，且该相关性依赖于模拟中黑洞吸积模型的选择（Bondi型 vs. 扭矩限制型）及晕质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究超大质量黑洞与宿主暗物质晕之间的物理联系，特别是暗物质晕结构（如浓度）是否影响黑洞质量增长，从而揭示星系-黑洞共同演化机制。

Method: 基于多个先进宇宙学流体模拟（TNG100、EAGLE、CAMELS-TNG、SIMBA），统计分析中心星系中黑洞质量与暗物质晕浓度（在固定晕质量下）的偏相关性，并对比不同黑洞吸积模型（Bondi vs. 扭矩限制）的影响。

Result: 在采用Bondi吸积模型的TNG100、EAGLE和CAMELS-TNG中发现显著正相关（r=0.24–0.66，p<10^-10）；该相关性在低质量晕中为负或不显著，高质量晕中转为强正相关；而在采用扭矩限制吸积的SIMBA中无显著相关（r=0.01）。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕浓度是调控黑洞-星系共同演化的一个基本参数，其影响通过中心气体密度结构调制Bondi吸积效率实现；黑洞吸积物理模型的选择显著影响模拟中黑洞与晕性质的统计关联。

Abstract: We report the discovery of a positive correlation between supermassive black hole mass and dark matter halo concentration at fixed halo mass in cosmological hydrodynamical simulations. Analyzing central galaxies in TNG100 (N = 18,954), EAGLE (N = 1,522), and CAMELS-TNG (N = 6,664), we find partial correlation coefficients of r = +0.24, +0.34, and +0.66 respectively, all highly significant (p < 10^-10). The correlation is absent in SIMBA (r = +0.01, p = 0.09), which employs a torque-limited black hole accretion model rather than the Bondi-based prescription used by the other simulations. Both TNG and EAGLE exhibit a mass-dependent sign transition: the correlation is negative or null at log(M200/Msun) < 11.5 but strongly positive at higher masses. We interpret this pattern as reflecting the coupling between Bondi accretion rates and central gas density structure: halos with higher concentration have denser cores, enabling more efficient black hole growth at fixed halo mass. The absence of the correlation in torque-limited models supports this interpretation. These results suggest that halo concentration may be a fundamental parameter governing black hole-galaxy coevolution.

</details>


### [117] [First-Principles Formalism for Simulating Self-Interacting Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.17998)
*Maria Ramos,Timothy Cohen,Mariangela Lisanti*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文挑战了暗物质数值模拟中一个标准假设，即宏观模拟粒子的相空间分布遵循与基本暗物质粒子相同的演化方程；作者针对频繁散射情形，首次从第一性原理出发，建立了微观粒子物理描述到宏观模拟粒子表示的映射，并揭示了模拟粒子间存在一种依赖于基本粒子散射截面的有效力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验暗物质数值模拟中‘宏观模拟粒子相空间演化与基本粒子相同’这一标准假设是否在强自相互作用（频繁散射）情形下依然成立。

Method: 基于第一性原理，构建微观粒子物理（自相互作用暗物质）到宏观模拟粒子（短平均自由程极限）的严格映射，推导出模拟粒子间的有效相互作用力及其等效散射截面。

Result: 证明该标准假设在频繁散射情形下不普遍成立；发现模拟粒子间存在源于微观物理的新型有效力，其等效散射截面由基本粒子截面决定。

Conclusion: 首次建立了从粒子物理参数到数值模拟参数的显式映射，为更准确地研究自相互作用暗物质对星系结构的影响奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: It is plausible that the dark matter particles have non-gravitational interactions among themselves. If such self interactions are large enough, they could leave an imprint on the morphology of galaxies. These effects can be studied with numerical simulations, which serve as the primary tool to predict the non-linear evolution of galactic structure. A standard assumption is that the course-grained phase-space distribution of the macroscopic simulation particles follows the same evolution equation as that of the fundamental dark matter particles. This Letter tests this assumption directly for the case of frequent dark matter scatterings, demonstrating that this is not generically true. Specifically, we develop a first-principles map from a microscopic particle physics description of self-interacting dark matter to a representation of macroscopic simulation particles for theories in the short-mean-free-path regime. Using this procedure, we show the emergence of an effective force between the simulation particles and derive their interaction cross section, which depends on the one from fundamental particle physics. This work provides the first explicit map from particle physics to simulation, which will facilitate exploring the phenomenological implications for galactic dynamics.

</details>


### [118] [Widespread Shocks in an Odd Radio Circle Host Galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18012)
*Alison L. Coil,David S. N. Rupke,Serena Perrotta,Saloni Agrawal,Cassandra Lochhaas*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过Keck/KCWI+KCRM积分视场光谱观测，发现ORC4中心星系中电离气体具有强[OII]发射、高速度梯度和弥散，且谱线比与激波电离模型吻合，支持其起源于产生射电环的激波事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Odd Radio Circles (ORCs) 是新发现的河外射电源，其起源未知；此前对ORC4中心星系的光学光谱已发现延展的[LINER型]电离气体，亟需更全面的多谱线空间分辨观测以揭示其物理机制。

Method: 利用Keck望远镜KCWI+KCRM仪器开展积分视场光谱观测，覆盖多个强光学发射线，分析电离/中性气体的空间分布、形态、运动学（速度场、速度弥散）及谱线比，并与激波和AGN电离模型对比。

Result: [OII]是该大质量年老星系中最强光学发射线，且比H-alpha等其他谱线更延展；气体运动学呈现显著空间不对称性、高速度梯度（>100 km/s）和高速度弥散（~200 km/s）；谱线比与200–300 km/s激波模型吻合，不支持AGN光电离主导。

Conclusion: ORC4中心星系中的电离气体极可能由激波电离产生，该激波事件很可能同时形成了大尺度射电环，为理解ORCs的物理起源提供了关键证据。

Abstract: Odd Radio Circles (ORCs) are a new class of extragalactic object, with large rings of faint radio continuum emission typically spanning 100s of kpc; their origins are unknown. Previous optical spectroscopy of the central galaxy in ORC4, a classic isolated ORC, revealed spatially-extended ionized gas with strong [OII] emission and line ratios consistent with LINER emission. We present new Keck/KCWI+KCRM integral field spectroscopy covering multiple strong optical emission lines to measure the extent, morphology, and spatially-resolved kinematics and line ratios of the ionized and neutral gas in the ORC4 central galaxy. We find that [OII] is the strongest optical emission line in this massive, old galaxy, and the [OII] emission is more spatially extended than other optical lines, including H-alpha. The gas kinematics show strong spatial asymmetries, high velocity gradients (>100 km/s), and high velocity dispersion (~200 km/s). The emission line ratios are most consistent with shock models with shock velocities of ~200-300 km/s and are not fit well by AGN photoionization models. These findings strongly suggest that the gas in the ORC4 central galaxy is the result of shock ionization in and around the central galaxy, likely associated with the event that created the large-scale radio ring of emission that identified this source as an ORC.

</details>


### [119] [Precision Spectroscopy for 1.9 Million Galaxies from SDSS-IV: Improved Spectral Measurements and Catalogs for eBOSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18076)
*Owen S. Matthews Acuña,Christy A. Tremonti,Kyle B. Westfall,Shea DeFour-Remy,Aleksandar M. Diamond-Stanic,Zach J. Lewis,Britt Lundgren,Drake Miller,Lizhou Sha*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文介绍了eBOSS数据处理流程（eBOSS-DAP），用于分析eBOSS DR17中近200万条高质量星系光谱，提供发射线、恒星与气体运动学、连续谱指数及恒星种群拟合等统一测量结果，并评估了光谱测光质量与测量可靠性，释放了全面的数据产品以支持星系演化和宇宙学研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: eBOSS光谱数据虽丰富，但此前主要服务于大尺度结构与重子声波振荡（BAO）测量，大量光谱信息未被充分挖掘；同时，大量重复观测为评估光谱测光质量提供了机会。

Method: 基于MaNGA-DAP适配开发eBOSS-DAP流程，对z < 1.12的1,899,553条高质量星系光谱进行统一分析，提取发射线流量与等效宽度、恒星与气体运动学、连续谱指数及恒星种群参数，并系统评估标定性能与测量可靠性。

Result: 生成了迄今最大规模的eBOSS星系光谱参数星表，量化了测量精度，发布了完整数据产品（含光谱测量、误差估计及质量标志），验证了eBOSS光谱的高测光一致性（重复观测偏差<3%）。

Conclusion: eBOSS-DAP成功释放了eBOSS光谱数据的全部科学潜力，为星系演化、星际介质物理及多波段交叉研究提供了高可信度、标准化的光谱数据库，推动后续时域与空间分辨研究。

Abstract: The Sloan Digital Sky Survey IV DR17 Extended Baryon Oscillation Spectroscopic Survey (eBOSS) consists of 2,233,939 high-quality optical galaxy spectra obtained through 2" fibers, providing a rich spectroscopic resource for studying galaxy evolution across a broad redshift range. eBOSS was designed primarily for large-scale structure and BAO measurements and, as such, focused on galaxy redshifts, leaving much of the information contained in the spectra unexplored. In addition to the trove of spectra, the large number of repeat observations (197,521 duplicate spectra) enables evaluation of the survey's spectrophotometric quality. To unlock this potential, we introduce the eBOSS Data Analysis Pipeline (eBOSS-DAP), adapted from the MaNGA-DAP, which delivers uniform measurements of emission-line fluxes and equivalent widths, stellar and gas kinematics, continuum spectral indices, and stellar population fits. Using the eBOSS-DAP, we successfully analyze 1,899,553 high-quality galaxy spectra below a redshift of $z < 1.12$ to produce an extensive spectroscopic catalog for the eBOSS galaxy sample. We characterize the calibration performance, quantify the reliability of the derived measurements, and release a suite of data products that fully exploit the power of the eBOSS dataset. These catalogs open the door to a new generation of studies in galaxy evolution and cosmology.

</details>


### [120] [Discovery of a Luminosity-dependent Continuum Lag in NGC 4151 from Photometric and Spectroscopic Continuum Reverberation Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18276)
*Hai-Cheng Feng,Sha-Sha Li,Mouyuan Sun,Ciro Pinto,Shuying Zhou,Yerong Xu,J. M. Bai,Elena Dalla Bontà,ZhongNan Dong,Neeraj Kumari,Jiaqi Lin,H. T. Liu,Kai-Xing Lu,Bin Ma,Ji-Rong Mao,Emanuele Nardini,Enrico Piconcelli,Fabio Pintore,Jian-Guo Wang,Ding-Rong Xiong*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过多波段反响映射观测NGC 4151，发现其连续谱滞后随波长呈τ ∝ λ^{4/3}关系但整体偏大6.6倍，并识别出巴耳末和帕邢跃变处的弥散连续谱（DC）污染；首次揭示DC成分存在本征Baldwin效应，且滞后-光度关系呈非单调性，表明滞后是吸积盘与宽线区共同贡献的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接约束活动星系核（AGN）吸积盘结构对理解超大质量黑洞增长及反馈机制至关重要，但长期多季光谱反响映射观测仍稀缺，尤其需分离吸积盘本征响应与宽线区（BLR）贡献。

Method: 对近二十年最亮态的NGC 4151开展高密度多波段反响映射观测，结合丽江2.4米望远镜光谱与Swift卫星紫外/软X射线协同监测，测量UV至光学波段的波长依赖连续谱滞后，并对比过去十年三次高精度监测数据。

Result: 测得滞后符合τ ∝ λ^{4/3}关系但比薄盘理论预测大6.6倍；在巴耳末和可能的帕邢跃变处发现明显弥散连续谱（DC）污染；三次观测揭示>3σ显著性的非单调滞后-光度关系；首次发现DC成分呈现本征Baldwin效应。

Conclusion: AGN连续谱滞后并非纯吸积盘信号，而是盘与BLR（含DC）共同作用结果；DC的Baldwin效应及非单调滞后行为对SMBH质量测量和吸积盘理论模型提出新约束。

Abstract: Accretion onto supermassive black holes (SMBHs) powers active galactic nuclei (AGNs) and drives feedback that shapes galaxy evolution. Constraining AGN accretion disk structure is therefore essential for understanding black hole growth and feedback processes. However, direct constraints on disk size remain rare -- particularly from long-term, multi-season spectroscopic reverberation mapping (RM), which is critical for isolating the intrinsic disk response from the broad-line region (BLR). We present results from an intensive multi-wavelength RM campaign of NGC 4151 during its brightest state in nearly two decades. This represents the third high-cadence monitoring over the past decade, capturing accretion states spanning the transitional regime between thin and thick disks, making NGC 4151 the only AGN with continuum RM observations across such a wide range in accretion states. Combining spectroscopy from the Lijiang 2.4 m telescope with coordinated Swift UV/X-ray monitoring, we measure inter-band continuum lags from UV to optical. The wavelength-dependent lags follow a tight $τ\propto λ^{4/3}$ relation, consistent with reprocessing in a thin disk, but exceed theoretical predictions by a factor of 6.6. Our lag spectrum reveals clear excesses near the Balmer and possibly Paschen jumps, confirming diffuse continuum (DC) contamination from the BLR. By comparing the three campaigns, we discover a non-monotonic lag-luminosity trend ($>3σ$), which cannot be explained by DC emission alone. We propose the lags reflect combined disk and BLR contributions, and present the first evidence that the DC component follows an intrinsic Baldwin effect. These results offer new insights into SMBH mass measurements and theoretical models of AGN inner structure.

</details>


### [121] [Measurements of quasar proximity zones with the Lyman-$α$ forest of DESI Y1 quasars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18281)
*Ryuichiro Hada,Paul Martini,David H. Weinberg,Zheng Zheng,J. Aguilar,S. Ahlen,D. Bianchi,D. Brooks,T. Claybaugh,A. Cuceu,A. de la Macorra,S. Ferraro,A. Font-Ribera,J. E. Forero-Romero,E. Gaztañaga,G. Gutierrez,J. Guy,H. K. Herrera-Alcantar,K. Honscheid,M. Ishak,R. Joyce,D. Kirkby,T. Kisner,A. Kremin,C. Lamman,M. Landriau,L. Le Guillou,A. Meisner,R. Miquel,A. Muñoz-Gutiérrez,N. Palanque-Delabrouille,W. J. Percival,C. Poppett,F. Prada,I. Pérez-Ràfols,G. Rossi,E. Sanchez,D. Schlegel,M. Schubnell,J. Silber,D. Sprayberry,G. Tarlé,B. A. Weaver,H. Zou*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用DESI第一年数据中超过10,000个近邻类星体对，研究前景类星体在z~2–3.5处对其背景类星体Lyα吸收的影响（横向临近效应），发现气体聚集效应强于电离效应，导致邻近视线方向吸收增强；推断出类星体周围IGM过密达Δ~10，但未观测到临近效应与前景类星体光度的显著依赖关系，暗示类星体辐射可能具有显著时变性或各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解类星体如何通过其环境和电离辐射塑造周围星系际介质（IGM），特别是‘类星体临近区’的尺寸与各向异性如何受其宿主晕质量、光度、年龄及辐射几何影响。

Method: 基于DESI Year 1中>10,000个投影距离r_⊥ < 2 h⁻¹ Mpc的类星体对，测量前景类星体对背景类星体Lyα吸收的横向临近效应，并分析该信号随投影距离和前景类星体光度的变化；在假设类星体电离光度各向同性且稳态的前提下，反演IGM过密度分布。

Result: 观测显示气体聚集主导电离效应，导致邻近视线吸收增强；推断出最亮类星体周围~1 h⁻¹ Mpc处IGM过密度达Δ~10；但未发现临近效应强度与前景类星体光度存在显著相关性。

Conclusion: 横向临近效应主要由高密度环境驱动而非电离辐射；光度无关性挑战了稳态各向同性电离模型，暗示类星体辐射可能存在显著时间变化或各向异性，或存在电离通量与气体密度的系统性抵消。

Abstract: The intergalactic medium (IGM) around quasars is shaped by their dense environments and by their excess ionizing radiation, forming a "quasar proximity zone" whose size and anisotropy depend on the quasar's halo mass, luminosity, age, and radiation geometry. Using over 10,000 quasar pairs from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) Year 1 data, with projected comoving separations $r_{\perp} < 2\,h^{-1}{\rm Mpc}$, we investigate how the proximity zone of foreground quasars at $z\sim2{\rm-}3.5$ affects Lyman-alpha absorption in their background quasars. The large DESI sample enables unprecedented precision in measuring this "transverse proximity" effect, allowing a detailed investigation of the signal's dependence on the projected separation of quasar pairs and the luminosity of the foreground quasar. We find that enhanced gas clustering near quasars dominates over their ionizing effect, leading to stronger absorption on neighboring sightlines. Under the assumption that quasar ionizing luminosity is isotropic and steady, we infer the IGM overdensity profile in the vicinity of quasars, finding overdensities as high as $Δ\sim 10$ at comoving distance $\sim 1\,h^{-1}{\rm Mpc}$ from the most luminous systems. Surprisingly, however, we find no significant dependence of the proximity profile on the luminosity of the foreground quasar. This lack of luminosity dependence could reflect a cancellation between higher ionizing flux and higher gas overdensity, or it could indicate that quasar emission is highly time variable or anisotropic, so that the observed luminosity does not trace the ionizing flux on nearby sightlines.

</details>

*Tanya Urrutia,Darshan Kakkad,Paula Sánchez-Sáez,Mojtaba Raouf,Swayamtrupta Panda,Sarah E. I. Bosman,Francisco Pozo Nunez,Annagrazia Puglisi,Sophia Flury,Dragana Ilic,Andjelka B. Result: 该巡天将成为首个在单一、变光与光谱联合框架下统一描述多样化遮蔽AGN种群的观测项目。
